date: "2018-07-05"
categories: type-theory

agda: true
---

This is my attempt to collect in just one-file, a basic overview of HoTT in Agda.
This source code was type-checked by Agda 2.5.4.

{: .references }

  - https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/
  - https://mroman42.github.io/ctlc/agda-hott/Total.html

Agda has a pragma to work with HoTT (`--without-K`):

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="438" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="442" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="450" class="Option">--without-K</a> <a id="462" class="Symbol">#-}</a>
<a id="466" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="471" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="478" href="Agda.Primitive.html" class="Module">Agda.Primitive</a> <a id="493" class="Keyword">public</a>

<a id="501" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#501" class="Function">_</a> <a id="503" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="505" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="509" class="Comment">-- trick for avoiding Agda module errors (jekyll)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Universes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type universe hierarchy. It hides Agda primitive
hierarchy and the keyword `Set`. It uses `Type` instead.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="782" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Universes"></a><a id="789" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#789" class="Module">Universes</a> <a id="799" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="808" class="Comment">-- Our Universe hierarchy. It is implemented over the primitive</a>
  <a id="874" class="Comment">-- Agda universe hierarchy but it uses Type instead of Set, the</a>
  <a id="940" class="Comment">-- usual name for the Universe in Agda.</a>

Types
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Empty Type

The empty type, representing falsehood.

### Unit

The unit type is defined as record so that we also get the η-rule definitionally.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1843" class="Comment">-- A record without fields is the unit type with a single</a>
<a id="1901" class="Comment">-- constructor.</a>
<a id="1917" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="⊤"></a><a id="1924" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1924" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1926" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1080" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="1934" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="1942" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="⊤.★"></a><a id="1954" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1954" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="unit"></a><a id="1957" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1957" class="Function">unit</a> <a id="1962" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1964" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1954" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a>

<a id="1967" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="1971" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> UNIT <a id="1984" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1924" class="Record">⊤</a> <a id="1986" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Basic types of Martin-Löf type theory and some basic
functions.

### Σ-types

Sigma types are a particular case of records, but records can be
constructed using only sigma types. Note that l ⊔ q is the maximum
of two hierarchy levels l and q. This way, we define sigma types in
full generality, at each universe.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2329" class="Keyword">infixr</a> <a id="2336" class="Number">60</a> <a id="2339" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2428" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>

  <a id="2416" class="Keyword">constructor</a> <a id="Σ._,_"></a><a id="2428" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2428" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_,_</a>
  <a id="2434" class="Keyword">field</a>

### Products (×)

Product type as a particular case of the sigma

### Boolean

Boolean type, two constants true and false

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3082" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="Bool"></a><a id="3087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3087" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="3092" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3094" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1080" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3100" class="Keyword">where</a>

* Booleans can be defined by using a coproduct.

### Natural numbers

Natural numbers are the initial algebra for a constant and a
successor function. The BUILTIN declaration allows us to use
natural numbers in arabic notation.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="3390" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="ℕ"></a><a id="3395" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3397" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1080" class="Function">Type0</a> <a id="3405" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="ℕ.zero"></a><a id="3413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3413" class="InductiveConstructor">zero</a> <a id="3418" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3420" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>
  <a id="ℕ.succ"></a><a id="3424" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3424" class="InductiveConstructor">succ</a> <a id="3429" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3431" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3433" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="Nat"></a><a id="3438" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3438" class="Function">Nat</a> <a id="3442" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3444" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a>

<a id="3447" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="3451" class="Keyword">BUILTIN</a> NATURAL <a id="3467" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3395" class="Datatype">ℕ</a> <a id="3469" class="Symbol">#-}</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


### Common functions

#### Identity function
The identity function with implicit type.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="id"></a><a id="3586" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3586" class="Function">id</a> <a id="3589" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3591" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="3593" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3594" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3594" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3595" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3597" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3598" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3602" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="3607" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3594" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="3608" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3610" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3612" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3598" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3614" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3616" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3598" class="Bound">A</a>

The identity function on a type `A` is `idf A`.

some errors for my jekyll configuration.

#### Instance Searh

### Identity Type

Equality is defined as an inductive type. Its induction principle
is the J-eliminator.

### PathOver

If you have a dependent type `B` over `A`, a path `p : x == y` in `A` and two
points `u : B x` and `v : B y`, there is a **type** `[u == v [ B ↓ p]]` of paths
from `u` to `v` lying over the path `p`.  By definition, if `p` is a constant
path, then `[u == v [ B ↓ p ]]` is just an ordinary path in the fiber.
[More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L115).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="PathOver"></a><a id="6329" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6329" class="Function">PathOver</a> <a id="6338" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6340" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="6342" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6343" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6343" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="6346" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6348" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6350" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6351" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6351" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6353" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6355" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6360" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6343" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="6362" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6364" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6365" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6365" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="6367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6351" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="6371" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6373" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="6378" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6346" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="6380" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="6485" class="Keyword">infix</a> <a id="6491" class="Number">30</a> <a id="6494" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6329" class="Function">PathOver</a>
<a id="6503" class="Keyword">syntax</a> <a id="6510" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#6329" class="Function">PathOver</a> B p u v <a id="6527" class="Symbol">=</a> u == v [ B ↓ p ]{% endraw %}</pre>

## Equational Reasoning

Equational reasoning is a way to write readable chains of equalities.
The idea is that you can write the following:

{% raw %}
```agda
  t : a == e
  t = a =⟨ p ⟩
      b =⟨ q ⟩
      c =⟨ r ⟩
      d =⟨ s ⟩
      e ∎
```
{% endraw %}

where `p` is a path from `a` to `b`, `q` is a path from `b` to `c`, and so on.
You often have to apply some equality in some context, for instance `p` could be
`ap ctx thm` where `thm` is the interesting theorem used to prove that `a` is
equal to `b`, and `ctx` is the context. [More info here](https://github.com/HoTT/HoTT-Agda/blob/master/core/lib/Base.agda#L270).

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7201" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="EquationalReasoning"></a><a id="7208" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7208" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a> <a id="7228" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7229" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7229" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7231" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7233" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7234" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7234" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="7236" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7238" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="7243" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7229" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="7245" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7247" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="7256" class="Comment">-- Common combinators for equational reasoning. They allow us to</a>
  <a id="7323" class="Comment">-- write proof in an equational style. These versions have been</a>
  <a id="7389" class="Comment">-- adapted from the old version of the HoTT-agda library.</a>

<a id="7753" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="7758" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7208" class="Module">EquationalReasoning</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Actions on paths I

Properties and structure of the equality type.

### Equality

Types are higher groupoids.  If we see equalities as paths, this
is the inverse of a path. If we see equalities classically, this
is the symmetric property of equality.
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="inv"></a><a id="8057" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8057" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8061" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8063" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8065" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8065" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8066" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8068" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8069" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8069" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8071" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8073" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="8078" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8065" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="8079" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="8082" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8083" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8083" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8085" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8085" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8087" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8089" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8069" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8090" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="8094" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8096" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8083" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="8098" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8101" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8085" class="Bound">b</a>
  <a id="8105" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8107" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8085" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="8109" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="8112" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8083" class="Bound">a</a>
<a id="8114" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8057" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="8118" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8119" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5213" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8124" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8124" class="Bound">a</a><a id="8125" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8127" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8129" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5213" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="8134" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8124" class="Bound">a</a>{% endraw %}</pre>
Functions are functors to equalities.  In other words, functions
preserve equalities.

## Properties on the groupoid

<a id="9838" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="9843" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#8943" class="Module">·-Properties</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Transport

When we transport a proof of `(P a)` over an equality `(a == b)`, we
get a proof of `(P b)`.

                <a id="14210" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14212" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14213" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="14215" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14217" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14149" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14219" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14222" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14151" class="Bound">y</a><a id="14223" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14225" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14227" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14228" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14228" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14230" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14232" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14159" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14234" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14149" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14236" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14238" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14177" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="14240" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14149" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14241" class="Symbol">)</a>

## Homotopy

In a type-theoretical sense, a homotopy between two
functions is a family of equalities between their applications.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="14698" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Homotopy"></a><a id="14705" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14705" class="Module">Homotopy</a> <a id="14714" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14715" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14715" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14718" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14718" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14720" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14722" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14723" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14723" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14725" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14727" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14732" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14715" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="14734" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14736" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="14737" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14737" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14739" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14741" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14723" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="14743" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14745" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14750" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14718" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14752" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="14754" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="14762" class="Comment">-- A homotopy is a natural isomorphism between two functions, we will write</a>
  <a id="14840" class="Comment">-- f ∼ g when (f x == g x) for all x.</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.homotopy"></a><a id="14880" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14880" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14889" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14891" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14892" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14892" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14894" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14894" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14896" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14898" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14900" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14900" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14902" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14904" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14723" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14905" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14907" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14909" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14737" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14911" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14900" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14912" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="14915" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14917" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="14922" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14923" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14715" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="14926" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="14928" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14718" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="14930" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14934" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14880" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="14943" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14943" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14945" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14945" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14947" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14949" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14950" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14950" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14952" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14954" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14723" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14955" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14957" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14959" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14943" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14961" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14950" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14963" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="14966" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14945" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14968" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14950" class="Bound">x</a>

  <a id="Homotopy._∼_"></a><a id="14973" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14973" class="Function Operator">_∼_</a> <a id="14977" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14979" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14980" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14980" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="14982" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14982" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="14984" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14986" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="14988" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14988" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14990" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14992" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14723" class="Bound">A</a><a id="14993" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14995" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14997" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14737" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="14999" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14988" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15000" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="15003" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15005" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="15010" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15011" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14715" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="15014" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="15016" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14718" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="15018" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="15022" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15022" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15024" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14973" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15026" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15026" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="15028" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15030" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14880" class="Function">homotopy</a> <a id="15039" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15022" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15041" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15026" class="Bound">g</a>

  <a id="15046" class="Comment">-- Homotopy is an equivalence relation</a>
  <a id="Homotopy.h-refl"></a><a id="15087" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15087" class="Function">h-refl</a> <a id="15094" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15096" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15097" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15097" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15099" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15101" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15102" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15102" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="15104" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15106" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14723" class="Bound">A</a><a id="15107" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15109" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15111" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14737" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="15113" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15102" class="Bound">x</a><a id="15114" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="15116" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15118" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15097" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="15120" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#14973" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="15122" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#15097" class="Bound">f</a>

## Naturality

Homotopy is natural, meaning that it satisfies the following
square commutative diagram.

A particular case of naturality on the identity function.

## Fibers

## Equivalence

    <a id="18327" class="Comment">-- Contractible maps. A map is contractible if the fiber in any</a>
    <a id="18395" class="Comment">-- point is contractible, that is, each element has a unique</a>
    <a id="18460" class="Comment">-- preimage.</a>
    <a id="Equivalence.DefinitionOfEquivalence.isContrMap"></a><a id="18477" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18477" class="Function">isContrMap</a> <a id="18488" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18490" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18491" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18491" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="18493" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18495" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18290" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="18497" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18499" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18304" class="Bound">B</a><a id="18500" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18502" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="18504" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="18509" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18510" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18282" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="18513" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="18515" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#18285" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="18517" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="18571" class="Comment">-- There exists an equivalence between two types if there exists a</a>
    <a id="18642" class="Comment">-- contractible function between them.</a>

## Cartesian Product

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="21994" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="CartesianProduct"></a><a id="22001" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22001" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a> <a id="22018" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22019" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22019" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="22022" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22022" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22024" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22026" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22027" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22027" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="22029" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22031" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22036" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22019" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="22038" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22040" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="22041" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22041" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="22043" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="22045" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="22050" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22022" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="22052" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="22054" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="22063" class="Comment">-- In a pair, the equality of the two components of the pairs is</a>
  <a id="22130" class="Comment">-- equivalent to equality of the two pairs.</a>
  <a id="CartesianProduct.prodComponentwise"></a><a id="22176" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22176" class="Function">prodComponentwise</a> <a id="22194" <a id="22908" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="22913" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#22001" class="Module">CartesianProduct</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## DecidableEquality

A type has decidable equality if any two of its
elements are equal or different. This would be a particular
instance of the Law of Excluded Middle that holds even if we do not
assume Excluded Middle.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="23179" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="DecidableEquality"></a><a id="23186" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23186" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a> <a id="23204" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="23205" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23205" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23206" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="23208" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="23217" class="Comment">-- A type has decidable equality if we can prove that any two of its</a>
  <a id="23288" class="Comment">-- elements are equal or different.</a>
  <a id="DecidableEquality.decEq"></a><a id="23326" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23326" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23332" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23334" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23335" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23335" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23337" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23339" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23344" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23205" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="23345" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23347" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23349" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="23354" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23205" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="23358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23326" class="Function">decEq</a> <a id="23364" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23364" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="23366" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="23368" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23369" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23369" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23371" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23371" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="23373" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="23375" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23364" class="Bound">A</a><a id="23376" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23378" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="23380" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23381" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23369" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23383" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23371" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23387" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="23389" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2901" class="Datatype Operator">+</a> <a id="23391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#1675" class="Function">¬</a> <a id="23393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="23394" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23369" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="23396" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="23399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23371" class="Bound">b</a><a id="23400" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="23405" class="Comment">-- The product of types with decidable equality is a type with</a>
  <a id="23470" class="Comment">-- decidable equality.</a>

<a id="23891" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="23896" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#23186" class="Module">DecidableEquality</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## Propositions

Propositions as described on the main text. A type
is a proposition if we can create a function making any two of its
elements equal. We create a type of propositions.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="24126" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Propositions"></a><a id="24133" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24133" class="Module">Propositions</a> <a id="24146" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24155" class="Comment">-- A type is a mere proposition if any two inhabitants of the type</a>
  <a id="24224" class="Comment">-- are equal</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp"></a><a id="24239" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24239" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24246" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24248" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24250" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24250" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24251" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="24254" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24255" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24255" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24257" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24259" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24264" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24250" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24265" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24267" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24269" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24274" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24250" class="Bound">ℓ</a>
  <a id="24278" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24239" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24285" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24285" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24287" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24289" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24291" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24291" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24293" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24293" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="24295" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24297" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24285" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24298" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24300" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24302" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24291" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="24304" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#5166" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="24307" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24293" class="Bound">y</a><a id="24308" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24313" class="Comment">-- The type of mere propositions</a>
  <a id="Propositions.hProp"></a><a id="24348" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24348" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24354" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24356" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24358" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24359" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24361" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24363" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24368" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24369" href="Agda.Primitive.html#627" class="Primitive">lsuc</a> <a id="24374" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24358" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24375" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24379" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24348" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="24385" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24386" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24387" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24389" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24391" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2350" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="24393" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24394" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24399" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24386" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="24400" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24402" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24239" class="Function">isProp</a>


  <a id="24413" class="Comment">-- The dependent function type to proposition types is itself a</a>
  <a id="24479" class="Comment">-- proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.piProp"></a><a id="24497" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24497" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24504" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24506" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24508" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24508" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24511" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24511" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24513" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24515" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24517" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24518" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24518" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24520" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24522" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24527" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24508" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24529" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24531" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24533" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24534" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24534" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24536" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24538" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24518" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24540" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24542" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24547" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24511" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24549" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="24560" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24562" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24564" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24564" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24568" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24518" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24569" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24571" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24573" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24239" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24580" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24581" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24534" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24583" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24564" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24584" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="24587" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24589" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24239" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24596" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="24598" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24598" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24600" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24602" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24518" class="Bound">A</a><a id="24603" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24605" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24607" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24534" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24609" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24598" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24610" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="24614" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24497" class="Function">piProp</a> <a id="24621" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24621" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24627" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24627" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24629" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24629" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24631" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="24633" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20324" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="24640" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24642" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24642" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24644" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24646" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24621" class="Bound">props</a> <a id="24652" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24642" class="Bound">a</a> <a id="24654" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24655" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24627" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="24657" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24642" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24658" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24660" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24661" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24629" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="24663" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24642" class="Bound">a</a><a id="24664" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="24669" class="Comment">-- The product of propositions is itself a proposition.</a>
  <a id="Propositions.isProp-prod"></a><a id="24727" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24727" class="Function">isProp-prod</a> <a id="24739" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24741" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="24743" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24743" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="24746" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24746" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24748" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24750" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24752" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24753" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24753" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24755" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24757" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24762" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24743" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="24764" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24766" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24768" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24769" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24769" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24771" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24773" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="24778" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24746" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="24780" class="Symbol">}</a>
              <a id="24796" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24798" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24239" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24805" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24753" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24807" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24809" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24239" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24816" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24769" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="24818" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24820" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24239" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="24827" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24828" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24753" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="24830" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2726" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="24832" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24769" class="Bound">B</a><a id="24833" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="24897" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="24902" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#24133" class="Module">Propositions</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Sets

Sets are types without any higher dimensional structure, all
parallel paths are homotopic and the homotopy is given by a
continuous function on the two paths.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="25110" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Sets"></a><a id="25117" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25117" class="Module">Sets</a> <a id="25122" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25131" class="Comment">-- A type is a &quot;set&quot; by definition if any two equalities on the type</a>
  <a id="25202" class="Comment">-- are equal.</a>

             <a id="25478" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25480" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25218" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25486" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25436" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25488" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25490" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25218" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25496" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25452" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="25498" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="25500" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25218" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="25506" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25507" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25436" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="25509" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2726" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="25511" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25452" class="Bound">B</a><a id="25512" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="25817" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="25822" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#25117" class="Module">Sets</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

## HLevels

Higher levels of the homotopical structure, where the
first levels are:

- Contractible types (0)
- Propositions (1)
- Sets (2)

They would correspond to homotopy levels. We only work with
these first levels.

## EquivalenceProp

Equivalence of two types is a proposition
Moreover, equivalences preserve propositions.

<a id="28085" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="28090" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#27303" class="Module">EquivalenceProp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Half-Adjoints

Half-adjoints are an auxiliary notion that helps us
to define a suitable notion of equivalence, meaning that it is a
proposition and that it captures the usual notion of equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="28334" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Halfadjoints"></a><a id="28341" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28341" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a> <a id="28354" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28355" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28355" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28358" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28358" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28360" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28362" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28363" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28363" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28365" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28367" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28372" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28355" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="28374" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28376" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="28377" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28377" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="28379" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28381" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28386" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28358" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28388" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="28390" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="28399" class="Comment">-- Half adjoint equivalence.</a>
  <a id="28430" class="Keyword">record</a> <a id="Halfadjoints.ishae"></a><a id="28437" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28437" class="Record">ishae</a> <a id="28443" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28444" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28444" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="28446" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28448" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28363" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="28450" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="28452" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28377" class="Bound">B</a><a id="28453" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28455" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="28457" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="28462" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="28463" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28355" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="28466" href="Agda.Primitive.html#657" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="28468" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28358" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="28470" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="28472" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="31012" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="31017" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#28341" class="Module">Halfadjoints</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Quasiinverses

Two functions are quasiinverses if we can construct
a function providing gfx = x and fgy = y for any given x and y.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="31191" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Quasiinverses"></a><a id="31198" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31198" class="Module">Quasiinverses</a> <a id="31212" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31213" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31213" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a> <a id="31216" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31216" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31218" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31220" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31221" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31221" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31223" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31225" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31230" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31213" class="Bound">ℓᵢ</a><a id="31232" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31234" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31235" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31235" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="31237" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31239" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="31244" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#31216" class="Bound">ℓⱼ</a><a id="31246" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31248" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="33944" class="Comment">-- Half-adjoint equivalences are quasiinverses.</a>

     <a id="35408" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2444" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35412" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35413" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35021" class="Function">invEqv</a> <a id="35420" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35335" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35421" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35423" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#4058" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="35425" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#2444" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="35429" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35335" class="Bound">α</a>     <a id="35435" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7546" class="Function Operator">==⟨</a> <a id="35439" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#20324" class="Function">funext</a> <a id="35446" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="35447" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#19593" class="Function">rlmap-inverse-h</a> <a id="35463" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35335" class="Bound">α</a><a id="35464" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="35466" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7546" class="Function Operator">⟩</a>
     <a id="35473" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#3586" class="Function">id</a>
   <a id="35479" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#7645" class="Function Operator">∎</a><a id="35480" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="35483" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="35488" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#34229" class="Module">EquivalenceComposition</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Univalence

Voevodsky's univalence axiom is postulated. It induces
an equality between any two equivalent types. Some β and η rules
are provided.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="35687" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Univalence"></a><a id="35694" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35694" class="Module">Univalence</a> <a id="35705" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="35749" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="UnivalenceAxiom"></a><a id="35756" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35756" class="Module">UnivalenceAxiom</a> <a id="35772" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35773" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35773" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35774" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35776" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="35777" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35777" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="35779" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35779" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="35781" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="35783" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#982" class="Function">Type</a> <a id="35788" href="{% endraw %}{% link _posts/2018-07-05-hott-lib.md %}{% raw %}#35773" class="Bound">ℓ</a><a id="35789" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="35791" class="Keyword">where</a>

Somme lemmas about Univelance

{: .foldable}
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="36590" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36593" class="Comment">--   module UnivalenceLemmas {ℓ} where</a>
<a id="36632" class="Comment">--     -- The identity equivalence creates the trivial path.</a>
<a id="36693" class="Comment">--     ua-id : {A : Type ℓ} → ua idEqv == refl A</a>
<a id="36742" class="Comment">--     ua-id {A} =</a>
<a id="36761" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="36776" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv              ==⟨ ap ua (sameEqv (refl id)) ⟩</a>
<a id="36841" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (refl A)) ==⟨ ua-η (refl A) ⟩</a>
<a id="36894" class="Comment">--         refl A</a>
<a id="36912" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="36923" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="36926" class="Comment">--     -- The composition of equivalences is preserved into composition</a>
<a id="36998" class="Comment">--     -- of equalities.</a>
<a id="37023" class="Comment">--     ua-comp : {A B C : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → (β : B ≃ C) → ua (compEqv α β) == ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37119" class="Comment">--     ua-comp α β =</a>
<a id="37140" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="37155" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α β)                               ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv x β)) (inv (ua-β α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37262" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) β)                ==⟨ ap (λ x → ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) x))</a>
<a id="37367" class="Comment">--                                                            (inv (ua-β β)) ⟩</a>
<a id="37446" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β))) ==⟨ ap ua lemma ⟩</a>
<a id="37522" class="Comment">--         ua (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))                     ==⟨ ua-η (ua α · ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37605" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua β</a>
<a id="37628" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>
<a id="37639" class="Comment">--       where</a>
<a id="37654" class="Comment">--         lemma : compEqv (idtoeqv (ua α)) (idtoeqv (ua β)) == idtoeqv (ua α · ua β)</a>
<a id="37740" class="Comment">--         lemma = sameEqv (</a>
<a id="37769" class="Comment">--           begin</a>
<a id="37788" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua β)) ∘ fst (idtoeqv (ua α))                 ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="37876" class="Comment">--             (transport (λ x → x) (ua β)) ∘ (transport (λ x → x) (ua α)) ==⟨ transport-comp (ua α) (ua β) ⟩</a>
<a id="37986" class="Comment">--             transport (λ x → x) (ua α · ua β)                           ==⟨ refl _ ⟩</a>
<a id="38074" class="Comment">--             fst (idtoeqv (ua α · ua β))</a>
<a id="38117" class="Comment">--           ∎)</a>
<a id="38133" class="Comment">--</a>
<a id="38136" class="Comment">--     -- Inverses are preserved.</a>
<a id="38170" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua α · ua (invEqv α) == refl A</a>
<a id="38250" class="Comment">--     ua-inv-r α =</a>
<a id="38270" class="Comment">--       begin</a>
<a id="38285" class="Comment">--         ua α · ua (invEqv α)      ==⟨ inv (ua-comp α (invEqv α)) ⟩</a>
<a id="38355" class="Comment">--         ua (compEqv α (invEqv α)) ==⟨ ap ua (compEqv-inv α) ⟩</a>
<a id="38420" class="Comment">--         ua idEqv                  ==⟨ ua-id ⟩</a>
<a id="38469" class="Comment">--         refl _</a>
<a id="38487" class="Comment">--       ∎</a>

<a id="38501" class="Comment">--     ua-inv : {A B : Type ℓ} → (α : A ≃ B) → ua (invEqv α) == inv (ua α)</a>
